r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> dialect or probabilistic programming, where spinors and probabilities are natural.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Challenges</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Complexity</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Clifford algebra operations (e.g., geometric products) are computationally intensive, potentially slowing down MLIR passes.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Semantic Mapping</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Defining meaningful mappings from MLIR operations to multivectors requires careful design (e.g., what does a bivector represent?).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Tooling</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Existing MLIR infrastructure doesn’t support Clifford algebras natively, requiring custom implementations or libraries (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> in Python).</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">To prototype this in MLIR:</span></span></span></span><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><msub><mi>l</mi><mrow><mn>3</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>0</mn><mo it supports scalars, vectors, bivectors, and spinors.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 dependencies.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q <span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Define multivectors for CFG edges</span><span>
</span><span>edge_bb0_bb1 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.7</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.1</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> e1 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.2</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> e1 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">^</span><span> e2  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Probability, latency, dependency</span><span>
</span><span>edge_bb0_bb2 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.3</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.05</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> e1 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.1</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> e2 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">^</span><span> e3
</span><span>edge_bb1_bb3 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1.0</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.2</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> e1
</span><span>edge_bb2_bb3 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1.0</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.01</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> e2
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Adjacency matrix of multivectors</span><span>
</span><span>cfg_matrix </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> np</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>array</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> edge_bb0_bb1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> edge_bb0_bb2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> edge_bb1_bb3</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> edge_bb2_bb3</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Compute total probability (scalar parts)</span><span>
</span><span>total_prob </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sum</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>m</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> row </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> cfg_matrix </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> m </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> row </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> m </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">!=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Total probability: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">total_prob</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Sum of scalar parts (0.7 + 0.3 + 1.0 + 1.0)</span></code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Connection to Your Vision</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Your idea of "math as math as numbers" aligns perfectly with Clifford algebras, where program semantics (operations, control flow, dependencies) are encoded as multivectors—numbers with geometric structure. This unifies:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; I can suggest specific mappings.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Neural Operator Integration</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Explore how neural operators could learn multivector coefficients for optimization.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; I can provide:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System;
